            function closeCookiesBanner() {
                MG_Utils.setCookie('cookiesBanner', 1, '/', 7);
                document.querySelector('.cookiesBanner').style.display = 'none';
            };

            function cookiesBannerSeen() {
                var rate = typeof getCookieAdvanced === 'function' ? getCookieAdvanced('gaProbabilityPercent') : null,
                    probabilityRate = rate ? (parseInt(rate)/100) : 0.01,  // Sample GA click event to 1%
                    probability = Math.random() <= probabilityRate;

                MG_Utils.setCookie('cookiesBannerSeen', 1, '/');

                if(typeof ga === 'function' && probability) {
                    ga('send',  'event', 'Cookie Banner', 'Impression', 'Banner Load', { nonInteraction: true });
                }
            }

            const cookiesBanner = document.querySelector('.cookiesBanner'),
                  bannerSeen    = MG_Utils.getCookie('cookiesBannerSeen'),
                  bannerClosed  = MG_Utils.getCookie('cookiesBanner');

            if(cookiesBanner && !bannerSeen && !bannerClosed) {
                cookiesBannerSeen();
            }
        </script>

    function loadThumbsLazyLoad() {
        var image = document.querySelectorAll('.js-preload'),
            thumbToUse = 'data-mediumthumb';

        for (var i = 0; i < image.length; i++) {
            var itemsCount  = image[i];

            if (itemsCount.src != itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse)) {
                itemsCount.src = itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse);
            }

            if (i == 10) {
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    loadThumbsLazyLoad();

    // Thumbnail fetching:
    function loadThumbs() {
        var image = document.querySelectorAll('.js-preload'),
            thumbToUse = 'data-mediumthumb';
        for (var i = 0; i < image.length; i++) {
            var itemsCount = image[i];
            if (itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse)) {
                if (itemsCount.src != itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse)) {
                    itemsCount.src = itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse);
                }
            }
        }
    }
